C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L5:' Form: Linkkien vaihto (Link Updater)
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L6:' Purpose: Update linked table paths to current database directory
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L7:' Updated: 2025-11-12 - Added VBA7/64-bit support
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L9:' Description:
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L10:'   Utility form to relink external tables to the current database directory:
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L11:'   - Scans MSysObjects for linked tables
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L12:'   - Extracts database filename from current link path
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L13:'   - Relinks table to same filename in current database folder
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L14:'   - Prevents links to wrong directory after database moves
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L16:' Dependencies:
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L17:'   - MSysObjects system table (Access internal)
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L18:'   - Linked Access database tables
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L20:' Use Case:
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L21:'   When database is moved to new folder, linked tables still point to old
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L22:'   location. This form updates all links to current directory.
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L23:'================================================================================
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L25:'--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L26:' Event: Command0_Click
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L27:' Purpose: Relink all external tables to current database directory
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L29:' Process:
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L30:'   1. Get current database path (directory only)
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L31:'   2. Query MSysObjects for all linked tables
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L32:'   3. For each linked table:
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L33:'      - Extract filename from current link path
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L34:'      - Compare directory paths
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L35:'      - If paths differ, drop and recreate link to current directory
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L36:'   4. Preserve table name and structure
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L38:' Notes:
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L39:'   - Only relinks if source directory differs from current directory
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L40:'   - Uses case-insensitive path comparison
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L41:'   - Prevents duplicate relinking of same table
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L42:'   - Uses DoCmd.TransferDatabase to recreate links
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L43:'--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L57:' Initialize counter
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L60:' Get current database directory path
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L64:' Query for all linked tables
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L74:' Process each linked table
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L76:' Prevent processing same table multiple times
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L78:' Extract directory and filename from current link path
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L87:' Check if link path differs from current database path
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L91:' Drop existing linked table
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L94:' Recreate link to current directory
C:\database_migration\Access\PIPE\Form_Linkkien vaihto.cls:L107:' Cleanup
